font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2. 차인 것 :</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 의 동력에 의하여 도로에서 운전되는 것, 견인되는 차, 사람이 끌고 가는 손수</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 차가 아닌 것 : 전동차∙기차 등 궤도차, 항공기, 선박, 케이블카, 세발자전거, 유모차, 장</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1. 차가 아닌 것 :</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 애인용 휠체어</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">※ 사람이 끌고 가는 손수레가 보행자를 충격하였을 때에는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">차에 해당</span><span style="text-align: justify; </span>) : 의미의 강조</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">6. 고속도로 외의 도로를 통행할 수 있는 자동차</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 1차로 : 승용차, 중소승합, 1.5톤 이하 화물차</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 2차로 : 1차로와 동일함&nbsp; </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3차로 : 대형승합, 1.5톤 이상 화물차, 건설기계(덤프, 콘크리트믹서트럭 포함)</span> <br><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 4차로 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">특수, 이륜, 원동기장치, 자전거, 우마차, 건설기계(덤프, 콘크리트믹서트럭 제외)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp; ※ 고속도로를 통행할 수 있는 자동차&nbsp; </span><br><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1차로 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2차로가 주행차로인 자동차의 앞지르기 차로</span> <br><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2차로 : 승용차, 중소형승합차, 1.5톤 이하인 화물차</span> <br><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 3차로 : 대형승합차, 1.5톤 이상인 화물차</span> <br><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 4차로 : 특수자동차, 건설기계</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">7. 도로의 중앙이나 좌측을 통행할 수 있는 경우</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 일방통행 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 도로의 파손 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 도로공사 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑥ 교통정리 안하고, 좌우 확인 안 되거나 교통이 빈번한</span> </p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-size: 1px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 2px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 1px;">&nbsp;</span></p></td><td width="44" height="35" valign="center" style="border-width: 0.12mm 0.4mm 0.12mm 0.12mm; border-style: none solid none dotted; border-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);" colspan="4"><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 2px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 1px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 2px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 1px;">&nbsp;</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table><br><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한컴바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한컴바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13. 차마 서로간의 통행우선순위</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 긴급자동차(최우선 통행권을 갖는다)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 긴급자동차 외의 자동차(최고속도 순서)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 원동기장치자전거</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 자동차 및 원동기장치자전거 외의 차마</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">14. 긴급자동차의 특례</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 긴급 부득이한 때에 도로의 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">좌측 부분</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">을 통행할 수 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">일시 정지할 곳</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에서 정지하지 않을 수 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">자동차등의 속도, 앞지르기 금지시기, 앞지르기 금지장소, 끼어들기 금지장소</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에 관한 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 규정을 적용하지 아니한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">15. 비탈진 도로 또는 좁은 도로에서의 우선순위</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 비탈진 좁은 도로에서 자동차가 서로 마주보고 진행하는 때에는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">올라가는 자동차가</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 내려가는 자동차에게 도로의 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">우측 가장자리로 피하여 진로를 양보</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하여야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 좁은 도로 또는 비탈진 좁은 도로에서 화물을 실었거나 승객을 태운 자동차와 빈자</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 동차가 서로 마주 보고 진행한 때에는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">빈자동차가 도로의 우측 가장자리로 피하여 진로</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">를 양보</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하여야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">16. 운전면허취득 응시기간의 제한</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 운전면허를 받지 아니한 사람 또는 외국의 국제면허증 소지자가 결격기간 중 운전으</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 로 취소된 경우 : 위반일로부터 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2년</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 무면허 운전, 주취 중 운전, 과로(질병, 약물)운전으로 사람을 사상한 후 구호, 신고 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 조치를 아니하여 취소된 경우 : 위반일 또는 취소일로부터</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 5년</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 무면허 운전, 주취 중 운전, 과로운전 외의 사유로 사람을 사상한 후 구호, 신고조치</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 를 아니하여 취소된 때 : 취소일로부터 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">4년</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 주취운전 3회 이상 교통사고를 일으키는 경우 : 취소일로부터 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">3년</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑤ 주취 중 운전 3회 이상 위반으로 면허가 취소된 경우 : 취소일로부터 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2년</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑥ 위의 경우 이외의 사유(음주운전, 누산벌점 초과 등)로 면허가 취소된 경우 : 취소일</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 로부터 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1년</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑦ 운전면허 효력의 정지처분을 받고 있는 사람 : 그 정지처분 기간</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">17. 특례의 적용(</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">공소권 없는</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 교통사고)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">5년 이하의 금고 또는 2천만원 이하의 벌금</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 공소를 제기할 수 없다(</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">반의사불벌죄</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ※ 공소권 없음 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">'공소권 없음'이란 공소시효 경과, 고소권의 부존재, (친고죄에 있어서)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">고소의 취소 등으로 인하여 공소를 제기할 수 없는, 그러니까 재판에 회부하여 처벌할 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">수 없는, 경우를 말합니다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">18. 특례의 배제</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">종합보험(공제)에 가입되었고, 피해자가 처벌을 원하지 않아도 다음 경우는 특례의 적용</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">을 받지 못하고 형사처벌을 받아야한다(</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">공소권 있음</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">).</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">① 교통사고로 사람을 치사(사망)한 사고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">② 교통사고 야기 도주 또는 사고 장소로부터 옮겨 유기 도주한 경우</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">③ 다음의 중요법규 위반으로 사람을 다치게 한 때</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉠ 신호∙지시위반사고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">③</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉢ 속도위반(20km/h)과속사고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">③</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉣ 앞지르기의 방법․금지시기․금지장소 또는 끼어들기 금지 위반사고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">③</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉨ 보도침범∙보도횡단방법 위반사고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑦ 중안선 도색이 마모되었을 때</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧ 눈 또는 흙더미에 덮여 보이지 않을 때</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑨ 공사장 등에서 임시로 설치한 차선규제봉, 오뚜기를 넘어 사고 발생 시</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑩ 학교, 군부대, 아파트 등 단지 내 사설 중앙선 침범 시</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">22. 속도위반(20km/h초과)과속사고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">지정속도를 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">20km/h 초과된 경우</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">를 말하며 경찰에서 사용중인 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">속도추정방법은다음과 같다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">운전자의 진술</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">③ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); font-size: 13px;">②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 로 운전한 경우</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 건설기계를 제 1종 보통운전면허로 운전한 경우</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><div style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 면허 ? </span></div><div style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;</span></div><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">25. 음주운전에 해당되지 않는 사례</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 음주하고 운전을 하였다 하더라도 도로교통법에서 정한 주취기준에 해당되지 않으면 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 음주운전이 아니다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 경찰서, 군부대 등 교통이 통제되는 장소에서 음주한 채 운전한 경우에는 음주운전이 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 아니다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-size: 13px;"> ② 도로의 구부러진 곳</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 일반화물자동차 운송사업 : 일정 대수 이상의 화물자동차를 사용하여 화물을 운송하</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13. ① 일반화물자동차 운송사업 :</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 는 사업</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 개별화물자동차 운송사업 : 화물자동차 1대를 사용하여 화물을 운송하는 사업</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 용달화물자동차 운송사업 : 소형의 화물자동차를 사용하여 화물을 운송하는 사업</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">33. 책임보험계약 등의 계약종료일의 통지 등</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13. </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">보험회사 등은 자기와 책임보험계약 등을 체결하고 있는 보험 등 의무가입자에게 당해 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">계약종료일 30일 전까지</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 128); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">당해 계약이 종료된다는 사실을 통지하여야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">34. 운전업무 종사자격 결격사유</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 금치산자 및 한정치산자</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 파산선고를 받고 복권되지 아니한 자</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2)</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2)</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉡ 화물자동차운수사업의 진흥 및 발전에 필요한 통계의 작성 및 관리, 외국자료</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">13.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2)</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 의 수집∙조사 및 연구사업</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 화물자동차운송사업 및 화물자동차운송가맹사업에 이용되지 아니하고 자가용으로 사용</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 되는 화물자동차로서 대통령령이 정하는 화물자동차를 사용하고자 하는 자는 건설교통</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 부령이 정하는 사항을 시∙도지사에게 신고하여야 한다. </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">42.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> (※ 대통령령이 정하는 화물자동차</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">42.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">(※</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 특수자동차</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">42.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">(※</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 특수자동차를 제외한 화물자동차로서 최대적재량이 2.5통 이상인 화물자동차)</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 여객자동차운수사업법 및 화물자동차운수사업법에 의하여 면허∙등록∙인가 또는 신</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ 휘발유∙알코올∙가스 사용차 : 일산화탄소, 배기관탄화수소, 질소산화물</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;;
