font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 서 읽을 수 있는 사람의 시력을 말하며 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">정상시력은 20/20</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">으로 나타낸다. 예를 들어, </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">20/40</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이란 정상시력을 가진 사람이 40피트 거리에서 분명히 볼 수 있는데도 불구하고 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 측정대상자는 20피트 거리에서야 그 글자를 분명히 읽을 수 있는 것을 의미한다. 이 사</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 람은 정상시력을 가진 사람에 비해 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2배의 큰 글자를 제시</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">해야 같은 효과를 낼 수 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">63. 시각기준</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 제1종 면허 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">두 눈을 동시에 뜨고 잰 시력이 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">0.8이상</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">, 양쪽 눈의 시력이 각각 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">0.5이상</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 제2종 면허 : 두 눈을 동시에 뜨고 잰 시력이 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">0.7이상</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 다만, 한쪽 눈을 보지 못하는 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② 제2종 면허 :</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 사람은 다른 쪽 눈의 시력이 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">0.7이상이고 시야가 150도 이상</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 색채의 식별 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">적색, 녹색, 황색</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">의 색채식별이 가능하여야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">64. 동체시력</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">동체시력</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이란 움직이는 물체(자동차, 사람 등) 또는 움직이면서(운전하면서) 다른 자</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">동차나 사람 등의 물체를 보는 시력을 말한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 동체시력은 물체의</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 이동속도가 빠를수록 상대적으로 저하</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">된다. 즉 정지시력이 1.2인 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">사람이 시속 50㎞로 운전하면서 고정된 대상물을 볼 때의 시력은 0.7이하로, 시속 90</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㎞라면 시력이 0.5이하로 떨어진다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 동체시력은 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">연령이 높을</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">수록 더욱 저하된다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 동체시력은 장시간 운전에 의한 피로상태에서도 저하된다.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">65. 야간시력과 주시대상</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 사람이 입고 있는 옷 색깔의 영향 : 연구에 의하면, 무엇인가 있다는 것을 인지하는</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">데 좋은 옷 색깔은 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">흰색, 엷은 황색의 순</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이며</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 흑색</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이 가장 나쁘다. 무엇인가가 사람</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이라는 것을 확인하는데 좋은 옷 색깔은 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">적색, 백색</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">의 순이며 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">흑색</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이 가장 나쁘다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 통행인의 노상위치와 확인거리 : 주간의 경우 운전자는 중앙선에 있는 통행인을 갓길</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에 있는 사람보다 쉽게 확인할 수 있지만, 야간에는 대향차량간의 전조등에 의한 현</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">혹 현상으로 중앙선상의 통행인을 우측 갓길에 있는 통행이보다 확인하기 어렵다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">(무엇이 있다 : 흰색&gt;엷은 황색&gt;흑색,&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 무엇인가가 사람이다 : 적색&gt;백색&gt;흑색)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">66. 암순응</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 일광 또는 조명이 밝은 조건에서 어두운 조건으로 변할 때 사람의 눈이 그 상황에 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">적응하여 시력을 회복하는 것을 말한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 상황에 따라 다르지만 대개의 경우 완전한 암순응에는</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 30분 혹은 그 이상</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 걸리며 이</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">것은 빛의 강도에 따라 좌우된다(</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">터널은 5～10초 정도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">). 주간 운전시 터널을 막 진입</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하였을 때 더욱 조심스러운 안전운전이 요구되는 이유이기도 하다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">67. 명순응</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 일광 또는 조명이 어두운 조건에서 밝은 조건으로 변할 때 사람의 눈이 그 상황에 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">적응하여 시력을 회복하는 것을 말한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 상황에 따라 다르지만 명순응에 걸리는 시간은 암순응보다 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">수초～1분에 불과</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">68. 심시력</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 전방에 있는 대상물까지의 거리를 목측하는 것을 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">심경각</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이라고 하며, 그 기능을 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">심시</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 력</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이라고 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 심시력의 결함은 입체공간 측정의 결함으로 인한 교통사고를 초래할 수 있다.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">69. 시야와 주변시력</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 정지한 상태에서 눈의 초점을 고정시키고 양쪽 눈으로 볼 수 있는 범위를 시야라 한</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">다. 정상적인 시력을 가진 사람의 시야범위는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">180°～200°</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 시야 범위 안에 있는 대상물이라 하더라도 시축에서 벗어나는 시각에 따라 시력이 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">저하된다. 그 정도는 시축에서 시각이 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">약 3° 벗어나면 약 80%</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">, </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">6° 벗어나면 약 90%, </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 12° 벗어나면 약 99%</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">가 저하된다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">70. 속도와 시야</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 시야의 범위는 자동차 속도에 반비례하여 좁아진다. 정상시력을 가진 운전자의 정지</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">시 시야범위는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">약 180～200도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이지만, </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">시속 40㎞</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">로 운전중이라면 그의 시야범위는 약 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">, </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">시속 70㎞</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">면 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">약 65도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">, </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">시속 100㎞</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">면 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">약 40도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">로 속도가 높아질수록 시야의 범</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">위는 점점 좁아진다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">(정지 시 : 180~200도, 40km/h : 100도, 70km/h : 65도, 100km/h : 40도)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 한편 속도가 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">빨라질수록 가까운 곳의 풍경(근경)은 더욱 흐려지고 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">작고 복잡한 대상</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">은 잘 확인되지 않는다. 고속주행로 상에 설치하는 표지판을 크고 단순한 모양으로 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하는 것은 이런 점을 고려한 것이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">71. 교통사고의 원인과 요인</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 간접적 요인 : 교통사고 발생을 용이하게 한 상태를 만든 조건</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ 운전자에 대한 홍보활동 결여 또는 훈련의 결여</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉡ 차량의 운전 전 점검습관의 결여</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉢ 무리한 운행계획</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉣ 안전운전을 위하여 필요한 교육태만, 안전지식 결여</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉤ 직장이나 가정에서의 인간관계불량 등</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 중간적 요인 : 중간적 요인만으로는 교통사고와 직결되는 것은 아님(직접+간접요인=</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 복합적)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ 운전자의 지능&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡ 운전자 성격</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉢ 운전자 심신기능&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉣ 불량한 운전태도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉤ 음주, 과로 등</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 직접적 요인 : 사고와 직접 관계 있는 것</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ 사고 직전 과속과 같은 법규위반&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡ 위험인지의 지연</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉢ 운전조작의 잘못, 잘못된 위기대처 등</span> &nbsp;</p><div style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;</div><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">72. 착각</span> <span style="color: rgb(0, 40, 231);">&nbsp;</span></p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">① 크기의 착각 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">어두운 곳에서는 가로 폭보다 세로 폭의 길이를 보다 넓은 것으로 판단</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ② 원근의 착각 : 작은 것은 멀리 있는 것 같이, 덜 밝은 것은 멀리 있는 것으로 느낌</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ③ 경사의 착각</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉠ 작은 경사는 실제보다 작게, 큰 경사는 실제보다 크게 보임</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡ 오름 경사는 실제보다 크게, 내림경사는 실제보다 적게 보임</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ④ 속도의 착각</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉠ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">좁은 시야에서는 빠르게 느껴진다. 비교 대상이 먼 곳에 있는 것일 때는 느리게 느껴짐</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡ 상대 가속도감(반대방향), 상대 감속도감(동일방향)을 느낌</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ⑤ 상반의 착각</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉠ 주행 중 급정거시 반대방향으로 움직이는 것처럼 보임</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡ 큰 것들 가운데 있는 작은 것을 작은 것들 가운데 있는 같은 것보다 적어 보임</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉢ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">한쪽 곡선을 보고 반대방향의 곡선을 볼 경우 실제보다 더 구부러져 있는 것처럼 보임</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">73. 피로와 교통사고∙운전착오</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 장시간 연속운전</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 수면부족</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 운전착오는 심야에서 새벽 사이에 많이 발생한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">74. 보행자 사고의 실태와 요인</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 우리나라 보행중 교통사고 사망자 구성비는 미국, 프랑스, 일본 등에 비해 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.5～3배</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 며, 특히 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">어린이는 4～5배 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">정도 높다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 차대사람의 사고가 가장 많은 보행유형은 어떻게 도로를 횡단하였든 횡단중(횡단보</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 도횡단, 횡단보도부근횡단, 육교부근횡단, 기타횡단)의 사고가 가장 많다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 다음으로 어떤 형태든 통행중의 사고가 많으며, 연령층별로는 어린이와 노약자가 높</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 은 비중을 차지한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">75. 음주와 운전</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 매일 알콜을 접하는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">습관성 음주자</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">음주 30분 후에 체내 알콜 농도가 정점에 도달</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 하였지만 그 체내 알콜 농도는 중간적(평균적) 음주자의 절반 수준이었다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 중간적 음주자는 음주 후 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">60분에서 90분 사이</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에 체내 알콜 농도가 정점에 도달하였</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 지만 그 농도는 습관성 음주자의 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">2배 수준</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">이었다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 여자는 음주 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">30분 후</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에, 남자는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">60분 후</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에 체내 알콜 농도가 정점에 도달하였다. </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 이는 개인차를 고려하더라도, 성별에 따라 체내 알콜 농도가 정점에 도달하는 시간의 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 차이가 존재하며 여자가 먼저 정점에 도달한다는 사실을 시사한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px;
