font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 통의 원활한 소통을 도모하는 방법은 신호기를 설치하거나 교차로 자체를 입체화(입</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 체교차로 설치)하는 것이다. 이때 신호기는 교통흐름을 시간적으로 분리하는 기능을 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 하며 입체교차로는 교통흐름을 공간적으로 분리하는 기능을 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 교차로 황색신호시간은 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">통상 3초를 기본</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">으로 운영한다. 교차로의 크기에 따라 4～6초</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 까지 연장 운영하기도 하지만, 지극히 부득이한 경우가 아니라면 6초를 초과하는 것</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 은 금기로 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">99. 커브길</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">곡선반경이 짧아질수록 급한 커브길이 된다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 거크길에서의 핸들조작은 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">슬로우 인 패스트 아웃</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">(Slow-in, Fast-out) 원리에 입각하</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 여 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">커브 진입직전에 핸들조작이 자유로울 정도로 속도를 감속</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하고, </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">커브가 끝나는 조</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">금 앞에서 핸들을 조작하여 차량의 방향을 안정되게 유지한 후, 속도를 증가(가속)</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">50. ②</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 여 신속하게 통과할 수 있도록 하여야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100. 차로폭</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 차로 폭은 관련 기준에 따라 도로의 설계속도, 지형조건 등을 고려하여 달리할 수 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 있으나 대개 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">3.0m～3.5m</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">를 기준으로 한다. 다만, </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">교량위, 터널내, 유턴차로(회전차</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 로) 등에서 부득이한 경우 2.75m로 할 수 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 중앙선이 실선인 경우 중앙선침범이 적용되고, 중앙선이 점선일 경우 일반 과실 사</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 고로 처리된다.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">101. 철길 건널목</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 시동이 걸리지 않을 때는 당황하지 말고 기어를 1단 위치에 넣은 후 클러치 페달을 밟</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 지 않은 상태에서 엔진 키를 돌리면 시동 모터의 회전으로 바퀴를 움직여 철길을 빠져 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 나올 수 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; font-size: 13px;"> 요하다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 소나 돼지와 같은 가축 또는 살아있는 동물을 운반하는 차량은 무게중심이 이동하</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑦ 취급주의 스티커의 경우 운송장 바로 우측 옆에 붙여서 눈에 띄게 한다. </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑧ 화물수량은 원칙상 1개 화물에 1매 운송장 부착이므로 1개로 기입하되 다수화물로 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; font-size: 13px;"> 보조스티커를 사용하는 경우에는 총 박스 수량(단위포장 수량)을 기록한다. 이는 포</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 장 내 물품의 수량이 아니라 수탁 받은 단위를 나타낸다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">110. 포장의 개념</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">개장</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 물품 개개의 포장. 물품의 상품가치를 높이기 위해 또는 물품을 보호하기 위</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 해 적절한 재료, 용기 등을 물품에 가하는 기술 또는 가한 상태, 낱포장(단위포장)이</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 라 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">내장</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 포장화물 내부의 포장. 물, 습기, 광열, 충격 등을 고려하여 적절한 재료, 용</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 기 등을 물품에 가하는 기술 및 가한 상태, 속포장(내부포장)이라 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">외장</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 포장화물 외부의 포장. 물품을 상자, 자루, 통 따위의 용기에 넣거나 또는 용</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 기를 넣지 아니한 채 결속하고 기호, 표식 등을 가하는 기술 및 가한 상태, 겉포장</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> (외부포장)이라 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">111. 포장의 기능</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 보호성&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ② 표시성&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ③ 상품성&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ④ 편리성&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ⑤ 효율성&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ⑥ 판매촉진성</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">112. 포장기법별 분류</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">진공포장</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 주로 시품포장에 사용. 일반적으로 나일론 필름이 이용된다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">압축포장</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 수입면의 포장 등</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">수축포장</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 연신 플라스틱 필름의 열수축성을 이용하여 내용물을 수축성 플라스틱 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 필름으로 싼 다음 열을 가하여 수축시킴으로써 포장과 결속의 이중효과를 얻는 포</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 장으로서 작게는 병에서부터 크게는 트럭화물의 포장에까지 이용된다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">113. 창고 내 및 입출고 작업요령</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 하적단의 화물 출하시는 하적단 위에서부터 순차적으로 층계를 지으면서 헐어낸다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 하적단의 상층과 하층에서 동시에 작업을 하지 않는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 하적단 화물을 출하할 때는 하적단 위에서부터 순차적으로 층계를 지으면서 헐어내</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 고 층계의 높이는 가급적 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">1.5m이하</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">로 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">114. 하역방법</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 종류가 다른 것을 적치할 때는 무거운 것을 밑에 쌓는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 철강재 적치시는 열을 형성하되 길이 13m 이하는 2개의 받침목을, 20m 이상은 6개</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 의 받침목을 놓는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 포대하물의 하적단 높이는 지대 20단, 합성수지대는 10단으로 하고 중간에 종이 등</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 을 깔아 붕괴방지 조치를 취해야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 제재목을 적치할 때는 건너지르는 대목을 3개소에 놓아야 한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">115. 차량 내 적재방법</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 무거운 화물을 적재함 뒤쪽에 실으면 앞바퀴가 들려서 조향이 마음대로 되지 않아 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 위험하다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 무거운 화물을 적재함 앞쪽에 실으면 조향이 무겁고 제동시에 뒷바퀴가 먼저 제동</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 되어 좌∙우로 틀어지는 경우가 발생한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 화물 적재시 최대한 무게가 골고루 분산될 수 있도록 하고, 무거운 화물은 중간부분</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 에 무게가 집중될 수 있도록 적재한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 긴 물건을 쌓을 때는 끝에 위험표시를 하여 둔다.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑤ 화물 결박시 옆으로 서서 고무바를 짧게 잡고 조금씩 여러번 당긴다. 앞에서 뒤로 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 당기지 않는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑥ 지상결박자는 한 발을 타이어 및 차량 하단부를&nbsp; 밟고 당기지 않는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑦ 트랙터 차량의 캡과 적재물의 간격을 120㎝이상으로 유지해야 한다. (※ 경사주행시 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 캡과 적재물의 충돌로 인하여 차량파손 및 인체상의 상해가 발생할 수 있다.)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">116. 운송방법</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 단독으로 일시작업시 1인당 화물의 적정 무게한도(</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">성인남자 20～25kg, 성인여자</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">15 ~20kg </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">)를 준수한다.</span> </p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.<span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">②</span></span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 단독으로 계속작업시 1인당 화물의 적정 무게한도(</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">성인남자 10～15kg, 성인여자</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">5~10kg 정도</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">)를 준수한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">③</span> 두 사람이 운반작업을 할 때는 체력 및 신장이 비슷한 사람으로 조를 편성하고 화</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 물중량이 평균하게 걸리도록 하고 신호에 의하여 동작을 취한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">④ 장척물(긴화물), 구르기 쉬운 화물은 단독 운반을 피하고, 중량물(무거운 화물)은 하</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 역기계를 사용한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">117. 위험물 취급시의 확인점검</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 탱크로리에 커플링은 잘 연결되었는가 확인한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 플렌지 등 연결부분에 새는 곳은 없는가 확인한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 플렉시블 호스는 고정시켰는가 확인한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 인화성 물질 취급시 소화기를 준비하고, 흡연자가 없는가 확인한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑤ 주위에 위험표지를 설치한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">118. 팔레트 화물의 적재방식</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 밴드걸기 방식 : 쌓은 화물의 압력이나 진동∙충격으로 밴드가 느슨해지는 결점이 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 있다. </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 주연어프 방식 : 다른 방법과 병용함으로써 안전을 도모하여야 할 것이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 슬립멈추기 시트삽입 방식 : 부대화물에는 효과가 있으나, 상자는 진동하면 뛰어오</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 르기가 쉬워 문제가 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 풀붙이기 접착방식 : 방지대책의 자동화∙기계화가 가능하고, 코스트도 저렴한 방식</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑤ 수평 밴드걸기 풀붙이기 방식 : 풀붙이기와 밴드걸기의 병용이며, 화물의 붕괴를 방</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 지하는 효과를 한층 더 높이는 방식이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑥ 슈링크 방식 : 열수축성 플라스틱 필름을 팔레트 화물에 씌우고 슈링크 터널을 통과</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 시킬 때 가열하여 필름을 수축시켜서, 팔레트와 밀착시키는 방식으로서, 물이나 먼</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 지도 막아내기 때문에 우천시의 하역이나 야적보관도 가능하게 된다. 그러나 통기성</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 이 없고, 더구나 고열(120～130℃)의 터널을 통과하는 탓으로 상품에 따라서는 이용</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 할 수가 없고 또 비용도 높다는 결점이 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑦ 스트레치 방식 : 통기성은 없다. 비용이 높은 것이 결점이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑧ 박스 테두리 방식 : 팔레트에 테두리를 붙이는 박스 팔레트와 같은 형태는 화물이 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 무너지는 것을 방지하는 효과가 커지지만 평팔레트에 비해 제조원가가 높아진다.</span> <span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">119. 화물붕괴 방지요령</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 팔레트 화물 사이에 생기는 틈바구니를 적당한 재료로 메꾸는 방법</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> - </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">합판, 발포 스티롤판, 에어백</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">120. 하역시의 충격</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 하역시의 충격에서 가장 큰 것은 수하역시의 충격이다. 낙하충격이 화물에 미치는 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 영향도는 낙하의 높이, 낙하면의 상태 등 낙하상황과 포장의 방법에 따라 상이하다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 일반적으로 수하역의 경우에 낙하의 높이는 다음과 같다. </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ 견하역 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100㎝ 이상</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉡ 요하역 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">10㎝ 정도</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉢ 팔레트 쌓기의 수하역 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">40㎝ 정도</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">121. 보관 및 수송중의 압축하중</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 포장화물은 보관 중 또는 수송 중에 밑에 쌓은 화물이 반드시 압축하중을 받는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 이를테면 통상, 높이는 창고에서는 4m, 트럭이나 화차에서는 2m이지만, 주행 중에</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 는 상하진동을 받음으로 2배 정도로 압축하중을 받게 된다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">123. 제한차량의 표시 및 공고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px;
