color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 알면서 이를 숨기고 운송물을 인도한 경우에는 적용되지 아니한다. 이 경우에는 사</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 업자의 손해배상책임은 수하인이 운송물을 수령한 날로부터 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">5년간 존속</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 26px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 16px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 26px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold;">제4부 운송 서비스</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">146. 고객서비스의 형태</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">무형성</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 보이지 않는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">동시성</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 생산과 소비가 동시에 발생한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">인간주체(이질성)</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 사람에 의존한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">소멸성</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 즉시 사라진다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ⑤ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">무소유권</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 가질 수 없다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 40, 231); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">147. 고객만족을 위한 서비스 품질의 분류</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 상품품질</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 성능 및 사용방법을 구현한 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">하드웨어</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 품질이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 영업품질</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 고객이 현장사원 등과 접하는 환경과 분위기를 고객만족 쪽으로 실현하기 위한 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">소</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">프트웨어 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">품질이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 서비스 품질</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 고객으로부터 신뢰를 획득하기 위한 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">휴먼웨어</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 품질이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">148. 올바른 인사방법</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 머리와 상체를 숙인다(가벼운 인사 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">15°</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">, 보통인사 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">30°</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">, 정중한 인사 : </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">45°</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">).</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 인사하는 지점의 상대방과의 거리는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">약 2m 내외</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">가 적당하다. </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 약속할 때 허리는 건방지지 않을 만큼 자연스레 편다(상대방에 따라 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">10～15° </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">정</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 도 굽히는 것도 좋다).</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 128); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp; </p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">149. 호감 받는 표정관리</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">고객이 싫어하는 시선 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">: 위로 치켜뜨는 눈, 곁눈질, 한곳만 응시하는 눈, 위∙아래로 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 훑어보는 눈</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">교통사고 발생시 조치</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> : 어떠한 사고라도 임의처리는 불가하며 사고발생 경위를 육</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 하원칙에 의거 거짓 없이 정확하게 회사에 즉시 보고</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">150. 물류와 공급망 관리</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 1970년대</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉠</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 경영정보시스템(Management Information System) </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">단계</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉡ 창고보관∙수송을 신속히 하여 주문처리시간을 줄이는데 초점을 둔 단계이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 1980～90년대</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">전사적자원관리(Enterprise Resource Planning) </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">단계</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉡ 여기서 “전사적자원관리”란 기업활동을 위해 사용되는 기업 내의 모든 인적, 물</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉠</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 적 자원을 효율적으로 관리하여 궁극적으로 기업의 경쟁력을 강화시켜 주는 역</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉠</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 할을 하는 통합정보시스템을 말한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 1990년대 중반이후</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉠ </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">공급망관리(Supply Chain Management) 단계</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ㉡ 1990년대 중반이후 공급망관리 단계로서, 이 단계는 최종고객까지 포함하여 공급</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉠</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 체인상의 업체들이 수요, 구매정보 등을 상호 공유하는 통합 공급망관리 단계를 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">㉠</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 말한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">151. 물류의 개념</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">물류(로지스틱스 ; Logistics)란 공급자로부터 생산자, 유통업자를 거쳐 최종 소비자</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">에게 이르는 재화의 흐름</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">을 의미한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">물류의 기능에는 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">수송(운송)기능, 포장기능, 보관기능, 하역기능, 정보기능</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 등이 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ③ 물류라 함은 재화가 공급자로부터 수요자에게 전달될 때까지 이루어지는 운송∙보</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 관∙하역∙포장과 이에 필요한 정보통신 등의 경제활동을 말한다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ④ 최근 물류는 단순히 장소적 이동을 의미하는 운송의 개념에서 발전하여 자재조달이</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 나 폐기, 회수 등까지 총괄하는 경향이다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp; </p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">152. 물류의 역할</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">138.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ① 마케팅의 절반을 차지 : 물류가 마케팅 기능으로서 간주되기 시작한 것은 1950년대</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">⑧</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> 이다. 지금은 고객조사, 가격정책, 판매조직화, 광고선전만으로는 마케팅을 실현하기 </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;">100.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; font-size: 13px;"> 힘들고 결품방지나 즉납서비스 등의 물리적인 고객서비스가 수반되지 않으면 안 되</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ② 판매기능 촉진 : 물류는 고객서비스를 향상시키고 물류코스트를 절감하여 기업이익</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> ①</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;한양신명조&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> Right Quality (적절한 품질)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">크래프팅 </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">중심의 물류전략 : 특정한 프로그램이나 기법을 필요로 하지 않으며, 뛰어난 통찰력이나 영감에 바탕을 둔다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">157.물류전략의 실행구조</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; </span><span style="text-align: justify; line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">158.제3자 물류 : 화주기업이 고객서비스 향상, 물류비 절감 등 물류활동을 효율화할 수 있도록 공급사슬상의 기능 전체 혹은 일부를 대행하는 업종으로 정의되고 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">159.제3자 물류의 분류</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ①자사물류(1자 물류) : 화주 기업이 사내에 물류조직을 두고 물류업무를 직접 수행하는&nbsp;경우</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ②자회사물류(2자 물류) : 화주 기업이 사내의 물류조직을 별도로 분리하여 자회사로 독립시키는 경우&nbsp; </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ③3자물류 : 외부의 전문물류업체에게</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"> </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">물류업무를 아웃소싱하는 경우(장기적으로)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br>&nbsp; </p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">160.제3자 물류의 장점</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①물류산업의 합리화에 의한 높은 물류비 구조를 혁신</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ②고품질 물류서비스의 제공으로 제조업체의 경쟁력 강화 지원</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ③종합물류서비스의 활성화</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ④공급체인관리(SCM)도입∘확산의 촉진</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 255); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">161.제4자 물류 : </span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ①고객에게 제공되는 서비스를 극대화하는 것</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ②제3자 물류보다 범위가 넓은 서플라이 체인의 역할을 담당</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ③전체적인 서플라이 체인에 영향을 주는 능력을 통하여 가치를 증식시킨다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">162.제4자물류의 4단계</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"></span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①재창조 -&gt; ②전환 -&gt; ③이행 -&gt; ④실행</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">163.물류시스템의 구성</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; </span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">①운송 ②보관 ③유통가공 ④포장 ⑤하역 ⑥정보</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">164.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">공급망관리(SCM)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ①최종 고객의 욕구를 충족시키기 위하여 원료공급자로부터 최종소비자에 이르기까지 공급체인 내의 각 기업 간에 긴밀한 협력을 통해 공급업체인 전체의 물자의 흐름을 원활하게 하는 공동전략</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ②최종소비자의 손에 상품과 서비스 형태의 가치를 가져다주는 여러 가지 다른 과정과 활동을 포함하는 조직의 네트워크</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ③공급체인 관리에 있어서 각 조직은 긴밀한 협조관계 형성</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ④공급체인관리는 ‘수직계열화’와는 다르다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">165.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">전사적 품질관리(TQC)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ①제품이나 서비스를 만드는 모든 작업자가 품질에 대한 책임을 나누어 갖는다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ②불량품을 원천에서 찾아내고 바로잡기 위한 방안</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ③작업자가 품질에 문제가 있는 것을 발견하면 생산 라인 전체를 중단시킬 수도 있다.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ④문제점을 개선하는 것이며, 물류서비스 품질관리 담당자 모두가 물류서비스 품질의 실천자가 된다는 내용.</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">166.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">신속대응(QR)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ①생산,유통관련업자가 전략적으로 제휴-&gt;소비자의 선호 등을 즉시 파악-.시장변화에 신속하게 대응-&gt;시장에 적합한 상품을 적시에, 적소로 적당한 가격으로 제고하는 것</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp; ②신속대응의 효과</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉠소매업자 : 유지비용의 절감, 고객서비스의 제고, 높은 상품회전율, 매출과 이익증대</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉡제조업자 : 정확한 수요예측, 주문에 따른 생산의 유연성확보, 높은 자산 회전율</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ㉢소비자 : 상품의 다양화, 낮은 소비자 가격, 품질 개선, 소비패턴 변화에 대응한 상품&nbsp;구매</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">167.</span><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(255, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">효율적 고객대응(ECR)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp; 소비자 만족에 초점을 둔 공급체인관리의 효율성을 극대화하기 위한 모델</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">168.주파수 공동통신(TRS)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp; 무전기 시스템을 통한 꿈의 로지스틱스 실현</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">169.범지구측위시스템(GPS)</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;">&nbsp;&nbsp; 인공위성을 이용한 범지구측위시스템</span> &nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><br></span>&nbsp;</p><p style="margin: 0px; text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 21px; text-indent: 0px; font-family: &quot;바탕&quot;; font-size: 13px;"><span style="text-align: justify;
